Summary: [System][WiMAX] DUT become slowly after turn on WiMAX 

Do    : [Change]
            - Fix the CPU 100% issue.
               
        [Symptom]
            - 1. DUT become slowly after turn on WiMAX 
            
        [Cause]
            - 1. After check log, we found there are two thread make the CPU 100%.
			- 2. dm_detector_thread() and io_receiver_thread().
			- 3. The root cause is recvmsg() in while loop and make CPU busy.

        [Solution]
            - 1. Change the recvmsg() flag convert from blocking to non blocking

        [Notes]
            - None.

        [Expose]
            - None.

Team  : SW2-6-1-CONN
Issuer: Chris Deng
Mark  : SW6-2-1-CONN-CD-HOTSPOT_ENABLE_FIX-00
Issuekeys:[FB3.B-638]
Summary: Can't turn on hotspot after repeat turn on/off it for serveral times.

Do    : [Change]
            - Remove unnecessary driver load.

        [Symptom]
            - When WifiService want enable hotspot, it will first load station driver,
              and then unload it. Later, will load softAP driver.

        [Cause]
            - Between load and unload there has risk conditions.

        [Solution]
            - When we want to reduce time, and remove mWifiStateTracker.loadDriver().
              We also need setting wlan.driver.status is ok.
              BTWLANCOEX will release resource, so that can normal remove module.

        [Notes]
            - None.

        [Expose]
            - None.

Team  : SW2-6-Multimedia
Issuer: Jinju Hong
Mark  :
IssueKeys:[SF5.B-2308]
Summary: SBA porting for display driver

Do    : [Change]
            1. Update kernel/drivers/video/msm to SBA14
            2. Remove the solution for tearing effects in revisions 5847 and
               the modification in mdp.c (to disable/enable mdp vsync irq) in revision 7778,
               and set mdp_timer_duration as HZ (1 sec)
            3. Enclose set_backlight function with mdp_pipe_ctrl to prevent from
               writing mddi registers when mddi clock is disabled

        [Symptom]
            - None.

        [Cause]
            - None.

        [Solution]
            1. Update kernel/drivers/video/msm to SBA14
               1. SBA10
                  Disable/enable MDP/MDDI/Vsync clocks based on frame update
               2. SBA10#11
                  Set MDDI clock rate before enabling first time
               3. SBA10
                  Fix crashes in MDDI mode during fbtest/boot/suspend
               4. SBA12, CR 271317 & 271775
                  Fix MDDI blackscreen issue by vsync pending flag reset
               5. SBA13, CR 274480
                  Fix vsync timer deactivation by shutdown flag
               6. SBA13, CR 275229
                  Fix MDDI CRC Error handling condition
               7. SBA14
                  Enable S/W Vsync handler only if MDDI clock is enabled

        [Notes]
            - None.

        [Expose]
            - No.

Team  : Div2-SW5-Peripheral
Issuer: Owen Huang
Mark  : Div2D5-OwenHuang-FBx_Psensor_Pending_IRQ-00
IssueKeys:[FB3.B-826]
Summary: [Proximity sensor] Screen will flash some times after call connected when cover proximity sensor at first

Do    : [Change]
            -   When during phone call, system will set light sensor trigger interrupt time as 3200ms.
            After ending the call, system will set trigger time of light sensor as 200ms.
            
        [Symptom]
            -   Light sensor will trigger interrupt in phone call, and it would make system can't go to sleep.

        [Cause]
            -   Light sensor trigger interrupt too frequency.

        [Solution]
            -   Increasing trigger interrupt timer of light sensor during phone call. 

        [Notes]
            -   None.

        [Expose]
            -   None.

*-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
*       0.100.0351                                       2011/03/03 16:50
*-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
Team:   SW2-5-1
Issuer: Bryan Hsieh 
Mark: SW2-5-1-BH-ATAG_MEM-00
IssueKeys:[SF5.B-1914] [Market][Game] Angry bird would be closed or restart after suspend/resume device. 
Summary: [SF5.B-1914] [Market][Game] Angry bird would be closed or restart after suspend/resume device.  

Do    : [Change]
            - replace ATAG_MEM_RESERVED with ATAG_MEM for EBI1 memory region, in order to avoiding unstable memory allocation.
            - it will disable Dynamic Memory Management(DMM).

        [Symptom]
            - Launch angry bird and play it, then Suspend and resume device, Angry bird would be closed after suspend device. 
            
        [Cause]
            - Becasue appsboot pass ATAG with ATAG_MEM_RESERVED(hotpluggable memory which are not active during boot)
              to kenrel for EBI1 CS0 bank memory(the higher 256MB), it let EBI1 can enter deep power down mode when unplug(inatctived),
              that will enable DMM, so when DUT enter suspend mode, kernel inactive this memory region, 
              that casue physical memory is decreasing (That's why MemTotal is decreasing in /proc/meminfo),
              so LowMemoryKiller is working to kill process.
              Until DUT resume, this memory region is pluged(actived) from receiving a request from Android,
              The physical memory is increasing to orignial size.
                       
        [Solution]
            - replace ATAG_MEM_RESERVED with ATAG_MEM for EBI1 memory region,in order to avoiding unstable memory allocation.
            - it will disable DMM, so the physical memory won't be changed during suspend/resume.
            
        [Notes]
            - Becasue the EBi1 memory is not hotpluggable memory, it can't enter deep power down mode, 
              so the sleep current is higher than hotpluggable about 0.12mA.

        [Expose]
            - None.
            
Files :
		 * ./android/bootable/bootloader/lk/target/msm7630_surf/atags.c

*-----------------------------------------------------------------------------

*-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
*       0.100.0326                                       2011/02/24 17:27
*-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
Team  : SW2-5-2-Multimedia
Issuer: Seven Lin
Mark  : MM-SL-EndTTYCallWouldTriggerPTT-00
IssueKeys:[SF5.B-2130]
Summary: Fix- Music player open automatically when a TTY call was ended.

Do    : [Change]
            - Fix- Music player open automatically when a TTY call was ended.
            
        [Symptom]
            1.Make a TTY-TTY call
            2.The Music Player would be triggered automatically after ending TTY call. 
            
        [Cause]
            1. Headset mic_bias is disabled while ending tty_headset_mono_tx.
            2. If mic_Bias is disabled, PTT always would be high.
            3. If PTT is always high, it would be treated as headset button is pressed. 

        [Solution]
            1.It no need to handle PM_HSED_CONTROLLER_1 (headset mic_bias) in tty_headset_mono_tx.
            2.We have already control PM_HSED_CONTROLLER_1 with hedset plug/un-plug.

        [Notes]
            - None.

        [Expose]
            - None.

Files :
		   * ./android/kernel/linux/arch/arm/mach-msm/qdsp5v2/snddev_data_marimba.c

Team  : SW5-5-2-Kernel
Issuer: Stella Chen
Mark  :
IssueKeys:[SF6.B-944]
Summary: enable /proc/uid_stat interface to fix this issue.

Do    : [Change]
            -   enable /proc/uid_stat interface to fix 2 case in CTS are fail.
            
        [Symptom]
            -  two CTS cases failed,
            1) android.net.cts.TrafficStatsTest#testTrafficStatsWithHostLookup is failed
            2) android.net.cts.TrafficStatsTest#testTrafficStatsForLocalhost is failed

        [Cause]
            -  /proc/uid_stat is not enabled

        [Solution]
            - Enable CONFIG_UID_STAT flag in kernel configuration.
            Device Drivers -> Misc devices -> UID based statistics tracking exported to /proc/uid_stat

        [Notes]
            -   None.

            -   None.

*-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
Team  : Div2-SW6-2
Issuer: Money Chien
Mark  : Div2-SW6-MM-MC-PatchSBA07ForSF5_B_1891-00
IssueKeys:[SF5.B-1891]
Summary:

Do    : [Change]
            -   Patch SBA07 for SF5.B-1891 (opencore: Queue encoded frames in composer node port).
            
        [Symptom]
            -   Video which is recorded is very worse.

        [Cause]
            -   None.

        [Solution]
            -   Composer port checks remaining capacity in fragment writer queue before dequeuing an incoming encoded frame message.
            -   This will prevent frame drops at the fragment writer queue.
            

        [Notes]
            -   Since frames are held up in the composer port waiting to be written, this can cause lower fps in the recorded clip depending on file write speed.

        [Expose]
            -   None.

Summary: Porting SBA 10 RPC Router fix

Do    : [Change]
            - Porting SBA 10 RPC Router fix.
            
        [Symptom]
            - ARM9 fatal error due to CM m2a RPC timeout.
            
        [Cause]

              before resetting its flow control quota count to avaoid any possible race conditions.

*-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
*       0.100.0296                                       2011/02/18 11:53
*-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
Team  : Div2-SW6-2
Issuer: Chris Lu
Mark  : Div2-SW6-MM-CL-HDMI_Capture-00
IssueKeys:[FB0.B-3924]
Summary:

Do    : [Change]
            -   Fix issue FB0.B-3924
            
        [Symptom]
            -   TV screen would flash pink screen quickly while take a picture .

        [Cause]
            -   When change mode from preview to capture, camera HAL will free previewHeap first,
                and then allocate thumbnailHeap for postview. 
                So the thumbnailHeap may use the same pmem address which was used by previewHeap. 
                However, HDMI is still using old preview address to show frames, this make issues happened.

        [Solution]
            -   If HDMI is plugged in, allocate thumbnailHeap before clear previewHeap.
                initRaw() -> stopPreviewInternal() 

        [Notes]
            -   None.

        [Expose]
            -   None.

Files :
        * ./android/vendor/qcom/android-open/libcamera2/QualcommCameraHardware.cpp

Reviewer:
	Sendow Chen

IssueKeys:[SF4H8.B-16]
Summary: Enable lcm vregs and lcdc clocks in osbl instead of in appsboot

Do    : [Change]
            - Enable lcm vregs and lcdc clocks in osbl instead of in appsboot.

        [Symptom]
            1. It takes long time to turn on panel.
            2. Screen is blank in download mode.

        [Cause]

              These commands need amss to process.

*-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
*       0.100.0261                                       2011/02/10 18:45
*-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
Team:   SW2-5-1
Issuer: Bryan Hsieh 
Mark: None
IssueKeys:[SF5.B-1917] Add dump stack tool
Summary: Add dump stack tool

Do    : [Change]
            - It's a debug tool for process stack dump.
The stacklogs are saved in /data/stacklog/ with timestamp(_YYYYMMDD_HHMMSS) ex. stack_20100322_035143.
The maximum number of stacklog is predefined (20), it can be modified by -n parameter, the oldest one will be deleted when it's full.
Each stacklog will dump ps info first, then dump 
There are some general/error information in alog for help to check stacklog status, ex:
03-22 03:51:43.026 E/dumpstack( 1390): stack log files are more than 20, delete the oldest one
03-22 03:51:43.026 E/dumpstack( 1390): command:rm /data/stacklog/stack_20100321_102537
03-22 03:51:43.076 E/dumpstack( 1390): dump stack to /data/stacklog/stack_20100322_035143
03-22 03:28:15.306 E/dumpstack( 1354): can't find name:aaa

        [Symptom]
            - None.
            
        [Cause]
            - Driver impelementation needed.
            
        [Solution]
            - Add a executable program in /system/bin
            
        [Notes]
            - <usage>  dumpstack [-c] [-n rotate_number] [pids ... ] [pnames ...]
-c => Enable console output, if it's present,  it must be first one parameter
-n rotate_number => Define maximum number of stacklog (no more than 100), if it's present,  it must be first one or second parameter,
pids => Dump specific process stack info by pid, can be assigned multiple pids mixed with pnames  
pnames => Dump specific process stack info by pname , can be assigned multiple pids mixed with pids. 
          the pname can be substring in pname (stat or cmdline)

if there is no any pid or pname, it will dump all process stack
Ex: dumpstack -c -n 30 1 2 android 300 100 rpc
    dumpstack -c 
            
        [Expose]
            - None.
            
Files :

		 + ./android/external/klogd/dumpstack.c
		 * ./android/external/klogd/Android.mk
		 * ./android/system/core/rootdir/init.rc

        [Cause]

Team  : SW2-6-1-CONN
Issuer: Chris Deng
Mark  : SW2-6-1-CONN-CD-Property-04
        SW2-6-1-CONN-CD-reset9_patch-00
Issuekeys:[FB0.B-3819]
Summary: Device always show "Turning off" no reason when attemp to turn off Wi-Fi

Do    : [Change]
            - Update reset9 patch.

        [Symptom]
            - 1.Both FW and host driver have the fix for TPE hang (i.e. PHY Tx hang).
              2.FW changes to fix cmd53 write hang.

        [Cause]
            - None.

        [Solution]
            - 1.Starting a watchdog timer within the Phy Tx module with 16msec timeout for every transmission
                and if any transmission does not complete within 16msec Phy TX would reset itself and avoid staying
                in a hung state.
              2.- Delays of 300us @ 3 power up/down steps in FW.
                - Fix for nearing to Prev TBTT issue.
                - Disable receving Beacons when powering down to avoid races in PMU

        [Notes]
            - None.

        [Expose]
            - None.

        * ./android/vendor/qcom/proprietary/wlan/libra/firmware_bin/qcom_fw.bin

*       0.100.0224                                       2011/01/25 19:30
*-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
Team  : SW2-6-1-CONN
Issuer: Chris Deng
Mark  : 
Issuekeys:[FB0.B-2243]
Summary: The speed of download file via WiFi AP is slower than other DUT when download the larger file.

Do    : [Change]
            - Add gDataInactivityTimeout into qcom_cfg.ini file.

        [Symptom]
            - Download file via WiFi AP is slower than other DUT.

        [Cause]
            - If packets of arrival Time > gDataInactivityTimeout,
              DUT will loss packets and need re-receive again.
              This action will take a lot of time. And download will slower than other DUT.

        [Solution]
            - If gDataInactivityTimeout is not set, the default velue is 20ms.
              We set gDataInactivityTimeout=100 to avoid loss packets.

        [Notes]
            - None.

        [Expose]
            - None.

Files :
        * ./android/vendor/qcom/proprietary/wlan/libra/firmware_bin/qcom_cfg.ini

              and assign it to data structure.

						Part 1:
						-------            
  					static struct msm_gpio sdc4_sleep_cfg_data[] = {
						{GPIO_CFG(58, 0, GPIO_CFG_INPUT, GPIO_CFG_PULL_DOWN, GPIO_CFG_2MA), "sdc4_clk"},
						{GPIO_CFG(59, 0, GPIO_CFG_INPUT, GPIO_CFG_PULL_DOWN, GPIO_CFG_2MA), "sdc4_cmd"},
						{GPIO_CFG(60, 0, GPIO_CFG_INPUT, GPIO_CFG_PULL_DOWN, GPIO_CFG_2MA), "sdc4_dat_3"},
						{GPIO_CFG(61, 0, GPIO_CFG_INPUT, GPIO_CFG_PULL_DOWN, GPIO_CFG_2MA), "sdc4_dat_2"},
						{GPIO_CFG(62, 0, GPIO_CFG_INPUT, GPIO_CFG_PULL_DOWN, GPIO_CFG_2MA), "sdc4_dat_1"},
						{GPIO_CFG(63, 0, GPIO_CFG_INPUT, GPIO_CFG_PULL_DOWN, GPIO_CFG_2MA), "sdc4_dat_0"},
						};			            	
						
						Part 2:
						-------
						{
							.cfg_data = sdc4_cfg_data,
							.size = ARRAY_SIZE(sdc4_cfg_data),
							.sleep_cfg_data = sdc4_sleep_cfg_data, //Div251-PK-SD_SLEEP_table-00+
						},

*-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
*       0.100.0215                                        2011/01/24 13:35
*-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
Team  : Div2-SW5-MM
Issuer: Chris Lu
Mark  : SW2-5-CL-Camera-720P-00
IssueKeys:[SQ01.B-677]
Summary: Update camera 2030 SBA 07+08 

Do    : [Change]
            -   1.Update camera 2030 SBA 07.
                2.Update camera 2030 SBA 08.
            
            
        [Symptom]
            -   1.Potential Memory Leak in Gemini Driver.
                2.Abnormal postview with FXcamera application.
        [Cause]
            -   1.It did not free the memory for some cases.
                2.The preview size (and hence the postView size) aspect ratio is not matching
                  the picture size aspect ratio. So, the VFE logic is adjusting the postView size
                  in set dimension call and the adjusted values are not considered when 
                  allocating the postview buffer as the buffer is allocated before 
                  the set dimension call.
        [Solution]
            -   1.Free the allocated memory for all the cases.
                2.Calculate postview dimensions based on picture size aspect ratio
                 instead of using preview sizes. Call PRAM_DIMENSION ioctl before 
                 allocating the thumbnail buffers, beacuse this ioctl can return 
                 the updated thumbnail dimensions based on picture size aspect 
                 ratio and camera stack requirement.

        [Notes]
            -   None.

        [Expose]
            -   None.

        * ./android/vendor/qcom/android-open/libcamera2/QualcommCameraHardware.cpp
        * ./android/vendor/qcom/android-open/libcamera2/QualcommCameraHardware.h

Team  : SW2-6-1-CONN
Issuer: Chris Deng
Mark  : SW2-6-1-CONN-CD-UI_DELAY-00
Issuekeys:[FB0.B-3305]
Summary: DUT would lag 1-2 seconds when tap "connect" to an AP.

Do    : [Change]
            - Skip several times of scan.

        [Symptom]
            - DUT would lag 1-2 seconds when tap "connect" to an AP.

        [Cause]
            - Because of WCN1312 scan will take a lot of time.

        [Solution]
            - Skip several times of first scan.
              When ADD_NETWORK & SELECT_NETWORK, reset parameter of "scan_res_tried".
              This is used to speed up the first association if the driver
              has already available scan results.

        [Notes]
            - None.

        [Expose]
            - None.

Files :
        * ./android/external/wpa_supplicant_6/wpa_supplicant/ctrl_iface.c
        * ./android/external/wpa_supplicant_6/wpa_supplicant/scan.c

Team:   SW2-5-1
Issuer: Bryan Hsieh 
Mark: SW2-5-2-BH-EnhanceUI-00
IssueKeys:[SF5.B-1697] prevent user copy log to sd without reboot after disabling diag port related function
Summary: prevent user copy log to sd without reboot after disabling diag port related function

Do    : [Change]
            - Prevent user copy log to sd without reboot after disabling diag port related function

        [Symptom]
            - Some SQA forgot to reboot device after unckecking USB_QXDM_MODE, and still copy log to SD,
              it cause the efs log missing.
            
        [Cause]
            - SQA forgot to reboot device.
            
        [Solution]
            - when device happen the diag port related function is enable in "copy log to sd" function
              create system Property "dbgcfgtool.needreboot" and assign value to 1
            - If dbgcfgtool.needreboot = 1, can't copy log to sd excepter for reboot
            
        [Notes]
            - None.
            
        [Expose]
            - None.

*-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
*       0.100.0199                                       2011/01/19 18:56
*-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
Team  : SW2-6-Multimedia
Issuer: Jinju Hong
Mark  : SW2-6-MM-JH-Mddi_Panel-00
IssueKeys:[SF5.B-1477]
Summary: Port 2015 libgralloc-qsd8k to 2030 to fix SF5 graphics benchmark issue

Do    : [Change]
            - Port 2015 libgralloc-qsd8k to 2030 to fix SF5 graphics benchmark issue.

        [Symptom]
            - Many 2D and 3D graphics benchmark applications show that
              graphics performance of 2030 is worse than that of 2015.
              1. [SF5.B-1477] [KPI][System] Some result is worse than reference phone while using the An3DBench
              2. [SF5.B-1478] [KPI][System] Neocore result is worse than reference phone while using the Neocore
              3. [SF5.B-1479] [KPI][System] Some result is worse than reference phone while using the DroidBench

        [Cause]
            - In 2015, for LCDC panel, display loop can not release the buffer till another post happens.
              For MDDI panel, display loop should not lock the buffer.
              The codes for MDDI panel are removed in 2030 such that SF5 display loop locks the buffer improperly.

        [Solution]
            - None.

        [Notes]
            - None.

        [Expose]
            - No.

Files :
        * ./android/hardware/msm7k/libgralloc-qsd8k/framebuffer.cpp
        * ./android/hardware/msm7k/libgralloc-qsd8k/gralloc_priv.h

Reviewer:
        Sendow Chen

*-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
Team  : SW2-5-2-Multimedia
Issuer: Seven Lin
Mark  : MM-SL-AudioFTM-02
        MM-SL-OPControl-03
IssueKeys:[SQ01.B-672]
Summary: Fix- speaker1 and speaker2 would both play while only spk1/spk2 play

Do    : [Change]
            - Fix- speaker1 and speaker2 would both play while only spk1/spk2 play
            
        [Symptom]
            1.In FTM mode, SPEAKER1PLAYTONE, speaker1 and speaker2 would both playback.
            2.In FTM mode, SPEAKER2PLAYTONE, speaker1 and speaker2 would both playback.
            
        [Cause]
            - We never differ spk1 and spk2 before amplifier is opened.

        [Solution]
            1.If m_speaker_mono_left (SPEAKER1PLAYTONE), only open GPIO36(spk1)
            2.If m_speaker_mono_right(SPEAKER2PLAYTONE), only open GPIO37(spk2)

        [Notes]
            - None.

        [Expose]
            - None.

*       0.100.0174                                       2011/01/13 16:00
*-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
Team  : DIV5
Issuer: Jacky Chu
Mark  : SW5-Kernel-JC-Workaround_timing
IssueKeys:[SF6.B-715][Stability][Power cycle][System]DUT will shut down in suspend.
Summary: workaround timing issue.

Do    : [Change]
            - Add delay to workaround this timing issue.
			
        [Symptom]
            - If you suspend the device and wakeup by power key, system will reboot.
 
        [Cause]
            - If send keyevent(input_report_key()) to framework too fast, the system will crash.
			If change the timing(such as delay) the system is fine.
			Because other wakeup events timing are different, other key events don't cause this problem. 
 				 
        [Solution]
            - Add delay before send event to framework.
              
        [Notes]
            - Root cause still unknow.
			We just find out that timing will cause this problem.
                     
        [Expose]
            - None.

        * ./android/kernel/arch/arm/mach-msm/rpc_server_handset.c

Team  : SW2-5-1
Issuer: Pence Ko
Mark  : None
IssueKeys:[SF5.B-668]
Summary: Enable and confirm necessary kernel configure items.

Do    : [Change]
            - Enable and confirm necessary kernel configure items.
			
        [Symptom]
            - Some features may not work well.              
            
        [Cause]
            - Qualcomm default released version didn't enable these items.        
 				 
        [Solution]
            - Enable following kernel configure items.
              (Some of following items may already enable in previous configureation.)
              a. To meet Google CTS requirement.
              	-> Device drivers
              		-> Misc devices
              			-> UID based statistics tracking exported to /proc/uid_stat              
              	CONFIG_UID_STAT

              b. Speed up EXT3 filesystem Quadrant Advanced benchmark (reference FB0 project).
              	-> File system
              		-> Ext3 journalling file sytem support
              	CONFIG_EXT3_DEFAULTS_TO_ORDERED
              	
              c. Control Group support (reference FB0 project).
              	-> General setup
              		-> Control Group support
              	CONFIG_GROUP_SCHED
              		CONFIG_RT_GROUP_SCHED
              		CONFIG_CGROUP_SCHED
              		CONFIG_CGROUPS
              		CONFIG_CGROUP_FREEZER
              		CONFIG_CGROUP_CPUACCT
              		CONFIG_RESOURCE_COUNTERS
              		              	
              d. Enable VPN feature.
              	-> Device drivers
              		-> Network device support
              			-> PPP (point-to-point protocol) support              
              	CONFIG_PPP
              		CONFIG_PPP_ASYNC
              		CONFIG_PPP_DEFLATE
              		CONFIG_PPP_BSDCOMP
              		CONFIG_PPP_MPPE
              		CONFIG_PPPOLAC
              		CONFIG_PPPOPNS
              		
              	-> Networking support
              		-> Networking options
              	CONFIG_XFRM_USER
              	CONFIG_XFRM_STATISTICS
              	CONFIG_NET_KEY
              	
              	-> Networking support
              		-> Networking options
              			-> TCP/IP networking
              	CONFIG_INET_AH
              	CONFIG_INET_ESP
              	CONFIG_INET_IPCOMP
              	CONFIG_INET_XFRM_TUNNEL
              	CONFIG_INET_XFRM_MODE_TRANSPORT
              	CONFIG_INET_XFRM_MODE_TUNNEL
              	CONFIG_INET_XFRM_MODE_BEET
              	
              	CONFIG_CRYPTO_ECB
              	CONFIG_CRYPTO_ARC4              	
              	
              e. Make Apps can install to SD card.
              	-> Device drivers
              		-> Multiple devices driver support (RAID and LVM)
              	CONFIG_MD
              		CONFIG_BLK_DEV_DM
              			CONFIG_DM_DEBUG
              			CONFIG_DM_CRYPT
              			CONFIG_DM_UEVENT
              			
              	-> Cryptographic API	
              		-> Twofish cipher algorithm
              	CONFIG_CRYPTO_TWOFISH
              	CONFIG_CRYPTO_TWOFISH_COMMON													            	
            	   				              
        [Notes]
            - none.
        
        [Expose]
            - None.

*       0.100.0110                                       2010/12/30 15:23
*-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
Team  : SW2-5-1
Issuer: Pence Ko
Mark  : None
IssueKeys:[SF5.B-668]
Summary: Update gas gauge settings in DFI (2030 main).

Do    : [Change]
            - Update gas gauge settings in DFI.
			
        [Symptom]
            - Recharging temperature threshold set too high, and in most case
              the device cannot perform change after overheat.
            
        [Cause]
            - Some criteria are not well defined.
 				 
        [Solution]
            - The data mark inside DFI is 04-FIHSF5-2010122
            Settings changed:
            1. Temp Hys ==> 5dC -> 3dC                                 
            2. Delta Temp = 5dC -> 3dC                                  
            3. OT Chg ==> 45 -> 55                                 
            4. OT Chg Recovery ==> 40 -> 50                                 
            5. Taper Voltage ==> 50mV -> 25mV                                 
            6. BAT_LOW V ==> 3400mV -> 4000mV                                 
            7. SOC1 Set Threshold ==> 150 -> 143                                 
            8. SOC1 Clear Threshold ==> 160 -> 153                                 
            9. SOCF Set Threshold ==> 90 -> 72                                  
            10. SOCF Clear Threshold ==> 120 -> 102                                 
            	   				              
        [Notes]
            - none.
        
        [Expose]
            - None.

        * ./android/device/qcom/msm7630_surf/dfi/FIH_SF5.dfi

*       0.100.0107                                       2010/12/29 15:53
*-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
Team  : SW2-6-CONN
Issuer: Eric Chen
Mark  : Div2-SW6-CONN-EC-Channel13-01
IssueKeys:[FB0.B-212]
Summary: [WIFI] Support scanning channel 13 in Taiwan

Do    : [Change]
            -   Set g11dSupportEnabled=0
            -   Set regulatory domains JAPAN in qcom_wlan_nv.bin
            -   Modify WLAN driver to support this feature
            
        [Symptom]
            -   DUT can not find AP that uses channel 13.

        [Cause]
            -   DUT uses AP's becon to limit the scanning channel in 802.11d spec.
                If AP around DUT is FCC domain, DUT will limit scanning channel from
                channel 1 to channel 11. This behavior makes DUT not see AP set in 
                channel 13.

        [Solution]
            -   Disable 802.11d support. It makes DUT choose scanning channel from 
                regulatory domains in qcom_wlan_nv.bin

        [Notes]
            -   None.

        [Expose]
            -   None.

Files :
        * ./android/vendor/qcom/proprietary/wlan/libra/firmware_bin/qcom_wlan_nv.bin
        * ./android/vendor/qcom/proprietary/wlan/libra/firmware_bin/qcom_cfg.ini
        * ./android/vendor/qcom/proprietary/wlan/libra/CORE/SME/src/csr/csrApiRoam.c

Team  : SW2-6-1-CONN
Issuer: Chris Deng
Mark  : SW2-6-1-CONN-CD-SOFTAP_MAC-00
Issuekeys:[FB0.B-3168]
Summary: DUT could not connect to hotspot AP created by two FB0 DUT.

Do    : [Change]
            - Read 4678 of NV item is as soft AP mac address.

        [Symptom]
            - 1. Create two Wi-Fi hotspot (different SSID)
              2. try to connect to the two hotspot from other DUT
              3. DUT could not scan those two hotspots. It would only 
                 display one hotspot SSID on the Wi-Fi network list 

        [Cause]
            - Because of soft AP use default mac address from qcom_cfg.ini
              The two of DUT both use the same mac address.

        [Solution]
            - Because DUT is use unique mac address from NV item.
              At softAP mode, DUT can use it, not use default.

        [Notes]
            - None.

        [Expose]
            - None.

            1. In FTM mode, AUDIO MICRECORD ON/OFF, AUDIO MIC2RECORD ON/OFF, and
            HEADSET MICRECORD ON/OFF can not work.

                if ((file->f_mode & FMODE_WRITE) &&(file->f_mode & FMODE_READ))
            1-3.The test APP which 2030 FTM use copy from 2015, the test APP needs to have the 
                condition handle which is like 2030 APP:
                #ifdef AUDIOV2
	              afd = open("/dev/msm_pcm_in", O_RDONLY);
	              if (afd < 0) {
		            perror("cannot open msm_pcm_in");
		            close(fd);
	           	  return -1;
	              }
                #else
            2.  The audio dev_id for 2030 is not the same with 2015    

        [Solution]
            1. Change the test APP (mm-audio-native-test) for FTM use from 2015 to 2030.
            2. Modify audio dev_id for 2030 use. 
 

        [Notes]
            - None.

            - None.

*       0.100.0058                                       2010/12/16 22:00
*-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
Team  : Div5-BSP
Issuer: Chris Wang
Mark  : //SW2-D5-OwenHung-SF4Y6 keypad driver porting+
IssueKeys:[SF6.B-530]
Summary: Implement SF4Y6 keypad driver.

Do    : [Change]
            - Implement SF4Y6 keypad driver.

        [Symptom]
            - The key mapping were not correct, and the high/low active setting were different with FBx.

        [Cause]
            - Before, due to the SF6 keypad GPIO setting were the same with FBx, we use the same driver. 
				But we found : 
				The FBx keypad GPIOs were high active, that is : press keys --> GPIO value were HIGH. 
				Release keys --> GPIO value were LOW. 
				This is different with us, we decide to implement a new keypad driver for SF4Y6.

        [Solution]
            - Implement new keypad driver for SF4Y6.

        [Notes]
            - None

        [Expose]
            - None.

Files :
     * ./android/kernel/arch/arm/mach-msm/board-msm7x30.c
     + ./android/kernel/drivers/input/keyboard/sf6_kybd.c
     * ./android/kernel/drivers/input/keyboard/Makefile

     * ./android/kernel/arch/arm/configs/SF4Y6_defconfig

 		 + ./android/device/qcom/msm7630_surf/sf6_kybd.kcm
	 	 * ./android/device/qcom/msm7630_surf/AndroidBoard.mk

        [Symptom]

*       0.001.0171                                       2010/11/02   13:50
*-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
Team  : Div2
Issuer: Lio Chen
Mark  : Div6D1-LC-BSP-Porting_OTA_SDDownload-01
IssueKeys:[SQ01.B-478]
Summary: Porting OTA SDDownload 

Do    : [Change]
            -   1. Porting OTA SDDownload mechanism in recovery mode.
                   Modify Mount function and disable MTD function.
                2. Disable the function for convert NV_cust.xml to NV_cust.mbn.
            
        [Symptom]
            -   1. When update update.zip image in SD card, it will return fail.
                2. After update nb0 image in SD card, NV_cust.mbn will be in SD card.

        [Cause]
            -   1. FB0 project is eMMC boot and recovery mode mount function is for 
                   MTD function. When update update.zip image, it will mount system
                   partition fail.
                2. Now source code will build NV_cust.mbn therefore it do not need
                   to convert NV_cust.xml to NV_cust.mbn during OTA SDDownload.

        [Solution]
            -   1. Modify the mount function for eMMC device.
                2. Disable the mechanism for convert NV_cust.xml to NV_cust.mbn.

        [Notes]
            -   None.

        [Expose]
            -   None.

Files :
        * ./android/bootable/recovery/applypatch/applypatch.c
        * ./android/system/core/fih_img_update/fih_imgupd.cpp
        * ./android/bootable/recovery/updater/install.c
        * ./android/bootable/recovery/recovery.c

*-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
*       0.001.0169                                       2010/11/01 17:20
*-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
Team  : Div2-SW5-MM
Issuer: SendowChen
Mark  : Div2-P6-SC-Fix_CTS_Reboot-00,Div2-P6-SC-Fix_StaticBuild-00
IssueKeys:[FB0.B-1318]
Summary: Fix CTS reboot in Camera test item.

Do    : [Change]
            -   Fix CTS reboot in Camera test item.
            
        [Symptom]
            -   Sometimes device will reboot when testing CTS camera items.

        [Cause]
            -   Sometimes receive_jpeg_callback finishes its jobs after CTS ap calls camera HAL to release, 
            		in release function, the liboemcamera.so which is the caller of receive_jpeg_callback is released, 
            		and receive_jpeg_callback can't return to a valid code address, then tombstone occurs, 
            		and kernel panic is followed and device reboots.
        [Solution]
            -   1. Move lock() position to front side of receiveJpegPicture which is called by receive_jpeg_callback.
								2. Use static link build to combine code of liboemcamera.so into libcamera.so.

								In this committing, I use solution "1"; and also modify code for solution "2" to pass 
								the compiling error when DLOPEN_LIBMMCAMERA is set to 0 in Android.mk.

        [Notes]
            -   None.

        [Expose]
            -   None.

Files :
        * ./android/vendor/qcom/android-open/libcamera2/QualcommCameraHardware.cpp

Reviewer:

*-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
*       0.001.0158                                        2010/10/28 15:43
*-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
Team  : SW2-5-1
Issuer: Matt Peng
Mark  : 
IssueKeys:[FB0.B-1191]
Summary: (DbgCfgTool) Force close pccurs when copy log to SD card

Do    : [Change]
            -  Add android:configChanges="orientation" in TestOptions activity.
            
        [Symptom]
            -  DbgCfgTool force close.

        [Cause]
            -  there is a time cost ProgressDialog in TestOptions activity.
               If there's no configChanges setting to handle this, a configuration change occurs will shutdown current activity by default. 
               And we will get crashes because when the background thread is finished, it will try to change the state on the old one.
            
        [Solution]
            -  Add add android:configChanges="orientation" to the activity declaration in the manifest. 
               This attribute will prevent the activity from being restarted. Instead, the activity remains running and its onConfigurationChanged() method is called.

        [Notes]
            -  This especially happen in ProgressDialog.

        [Expose]
            -  None.

Files :
       * ./android/development/FIH/DbgCfgTool/GUI/AndroidManifest.xml

Reviewer:
        Ken Chen

*       0.001.0155                                        2010/10/28   09:20
*-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
Team  : Div6D1-BSP
Issuer: Lio Chen
Mark  : Div6D1-LC-BSP-Factory_reset-01
IssueKeys:[FB0.B-867]
Summary: Fix factory reset action can not work issue.

Do    : [Change]
            -   Add "devwait /dev/block/mmcblk0p9" into init.rc in recovery mode.

        [Symptom]
            -   During factory reset action, device will reboot into recovery mode but does not 
                do anything. 

        [Cause]
            -   In recovery mode, device can not mount cache partition (mmcblk0p9) and then it 
                can not get factory reset command file in this partition.

        [Solution]
            -   This is a timing issue. We add devwait command in init.rc file. Device will mount 
                cache partition after this partition is ready.

        [Notes]
            -   None.

        [Expose]
            -   None.

Files :
        * ./linux/android/bootable/recovery/etc/init.rc

            -   1. Disable home key interrupt during factory reset action in recovery mode.
                2. Fix partition rename issue after factory reset action.

        [Symptom]
            -   1. If user press home key during factory reset, device will stay in recovery
                   mode after action.

                   UUID.

                2. Factory reset does not specify partition name when erase userdata and cache 
                   partition.

        [Solution]

                2. Add partition name when erase userdata and cache partition.

Team  : SW2-5-2-Perpherial
Issuer: Owen Hung
Mark  : //SW2-D5-OwenHung-SF4Y6 keypad driver porting+
IssueKeys:[SF6.B-26]
Summary: Implement SF4Y6 keypad driver.

Do    : [Change]
            - Implement SF4Y6 keypad driver.

        [Symptom]
            - The key mapping were not correct, and the high/low active setting were different with FBx.

        [Cause]
            - Before, due to the SF6 keypad GPIO setting were the same with FBx, we use the same driver. 
				But we found : 
				The FBx keypad GPIOs were high active, that is : press keys --> GPIO value were HIGH. 
				Release keys --> GPIO value were LOW. 
				This is different with us, we decide to implement a new keypad driver for SF4Y6.

        [Solution]
            - Implement new keypad driver for SF4Y6.

        [Notes]
            - None

        [Expose]
            - None.

        * ./android/kernel/arch/arm/mach-msm/board-msm7x30.c

Team  : Div2
Issuer: Chris Lu
Mark  : Div6D1-CL-Camera-D1_WVGA-04
IssueKeys:[FB0.B-868]
Summary: Preview displayed abnormally after change the quality.


Do    : [Change]
            -   Preview displayed abnormally after change the quality.
            
        [Symptom]
            -   Setup Quality to HD(1280x720)->change Quality to MMS(250k).Preview displayed abnormally after change the quality

        [Cause]
            -   When change quality from 720P to MMS, camcorder release camera hardware and re-open it again. 
                This make sensor into standby mode and exiting standby mode with 720P, and then change resolution to VGA immediately. 
                After exiting standby mode, sensor needs some delay time before changing resolution.

        [Solution]
            -   Add delay time if needed.

        [Notes]
            -   None.

        [Expose]
            -   None.

Team  : SW2-5-1
Issuer: Matt Peng
Mark  : SW2-5-1-MP-DbgCfgTool-07*
IssueKeys:[FB0.B-593]
Summary: DbgCfgTool hanging in copy log to SD.

Do    : [Change]
            1. Modem crash logs have directly save to memory (0xF2000000), host don't need to use diag service to get these logs. (Reversion 1436)
                So we can disable original efs2log mechanism in FB0 project.
            2. Change Modem efs2log path to /data/efslog/OEMDBG_LOG for both APR and DbgCfgTool.
            3. Disable plog of FB400_FTM, SF4V5_FTM, SF4Y6_FTM.
            
        [Symptom]
            -  DbgCfgTool hanging in copy log to SD, it is because Modem doesn't save correct crash log in efs2 file system.

        [Cause]
            -  When DbgCfgtool try to send read efs2 request, diag service will hang in getlog() becasue of getting incorrect file name.
            
        [Solution]
            -  Disable efs2log through diag service.

        [Notes]
            -  None.

        [Expose]
            -  None.

*-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
*       0.001.0108                                       2010/10/06 18:30
*-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
Team  : Div2-D5-Peripheral
Issuer: Owen Hung
Mark  : //Div2D5-OwenHung-Silent Key GPIO shift+
IssueKeys:[SQ01.B-379]
Summary: SF4V5 Silent key GPIO number modify.

Do    : [Change]
            -   SF4V5 Silent key GPIO number modify.
            
        [Symptom]
            -   Silent key not work.

        [Cause]
            -   The usage of GPIOs on PMIC8058 were different in BSP1240 & 2015.
            Example:
			1. #define SILENT_KEY_GPIO 20 ---> #define SILENT_KEY_GPIO 19 (minus 1) 
			
			2. gpio_get_value(PM8058_GPIO_PM_TO_SYS(SILENT_KEY_GPIO) -1) 
				---> gpio_get_value(PM8058_GPIO_PM_TO_SYS(SILENT_KEY_GPIO) ) 
			
			3. if(PM8058_GPIO_IRQ(PMIC8058_IRQ_BASE, SILENT_KEY_GPIO) == irq) 
				---> no change, because the definition of SILENT_KEY_GPIO changed 
				
			4. pm8058_gpio_config(SILENT_KEY_GPIO -1, &gpiokpd_configuration) 
				---> pm8058_gpio_config(SILENT_KEY_GPIO, &gpiokpd_configuration) 
				
			5. gpio_request(PM8058_GPIO_PM_TO_SYS(SILENT_KEY_GPIO) -1, "silent_key") 
				---> gpio_request(PM8058_GPIO_PM_TO_SYS(SILENT_KEY_GPIO), "silent_key") 
				
			6. request_irq(PM8058_GPIO_IRQ(PMIC8058_IRQ_BASE, SILENT_KEY_GPIO), &pmic8058_gpio_irq_handler, (IRQF_TRIGGER_R	ISING | IRQF_TRIGGER_FALLING), SF4V5_PMICKPD_NAME, kp); 
				---> no change 

        [Solution]
            -   Modify the GPIO mapping number while using gpio_request, gpio_get_value, pm8058_gpio_config...etc

        [Notes]
            -   None.
            
        [Expose]
            -   None.

Files :
		* ./android/kernel/drivers/input/keyboard/pmic8058-keypad.c
		
Reviewer:
	Kevin Wang

Team  : SW2-5-1
Issuer: Matt Peng
Mark  : SW2-5-1-MP-DbgCfgTool-05
IssueKeys:[SQ01.B-328]
Summary: (DbgCfgTool) Cannot redirect alogs to sdcard.

Do    : [Change]
            - Set property EXTERNAL_STORAGE_STATE when Volumn daemon changes state.
            - Add Logcat Configurations - System menu in Logger Conf. to let us control system alog.
            
        [Symptom]
            - Cannot redirect alogs to sdcard after we change the alog path to sdcard.

        [Cause]
            - property EXTERNAL_STORAGE_STATE is no longer use in Froyo, DbgCfgTool redirect log path only when sdcard status is "mounted".

        [Solution]
            - Set property EXTERNAL_STORAGE_STATE when Volumn daemon changes state. The new state name is "Mounted".

        [Notes]
            - None.

        [Expose]
            - None.

            -   Fix the bug that PC-Tool can not use after enabling USB Tethering.
            
        [Symptom]
            -   None.

        [Cause]
            -   When device connect to PC, it can auto install driver.

        [Solution]
            -   None.

        [Notes]

        [Symptom]

Do    : [Change]
            . Fix FQC WiFi Test Tool
            
        [Symptom]
            . FQC WiFi test can not work at the first time we launch it. However, after we launch once, it
              can work.

        [Cause]
            . Because the WiFi framework in Android 2.2(Froyo) has something different from in Android 2.1, 
              there is a new state(That maybe exist in Eclair but never appears) 
              that FQC WiFi tool does not handle well.

        [Solution]
            . Take the same action as receiving SCAN_RESULTS_AVAILABLE_ACTION when FQC receives state 
              SUPPLICANT_CONNECTION_CHANGE_ACTION.

        [Notes]
            . None
